 if (newWindow)
 window.open(url, '_blank');
 else
 document.location = url;
 }

 var loadQueue = [];
 function runOnLoad(fn) { loadQueue.push(fn); }
 window.onload = function() {
 for (var i = 0; i < loadQueue.length; i++)
 loadQueue[i]();
 delete loadQueue;
 };

  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {

    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;

  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {

  }

    display: block;

  }

  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

  .medium-heading {

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<br>





Protection" template. For all other reports, please use a different



<b class="line"><!---->Protection" template. For all other reports, please use a different<!----></b>



<br>





template.



<b class="line"><!---->template.<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Please READ THIS FAQ before filing a bug: https://chromium.googlesource.com



<b class="line"><!---->Please READ THIS FAQ before filing a bug: https://chromium.googlesource.com<!----></b>



<br>





/chromium/src/+/HEAD/docs/security/faq.md



<b class="line"><!---->/chromium/src/+/HEAD/docs/security/faq.md<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->Please see the following link for instructions on filing security bugs:<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->https://www.chromium.org/Home/chromium-security/reporting-security-bugs<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->Reports may be eligible for reward payments under the Chrome VRP:<!----></b>



<br>





http://g.co/ChromeBugRewards



<b class="line"><!---->http://g.co/ChromeBugRewards<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->NOTE: Security bugs are normally made public once a fix has been widely<!----></b>

deployed.



<b class="line"><!---->deployed.<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->-------------------------<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





In the mojo interface ContentIndexService::GetDescriptions, it will go to function |ContentIndexDatabase::GetDescriptionsOnCoreThread|:



<span class="line"><!---->In the mojo interface ContentIndexService::GetDescriptions, it will go to function |ContentIndexDatabase::GetDescriptionsOnCoreThread|:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





"""



<span class="line"><!---->"""<!----></span>



<br>





  service_worker_context_->GetRegistrationUserDataByKeyPrefix(



<span class="line"><!---->  service_worker_context_-&gt;GetRegistrationUserDataByKeyPrefix(<!----></span>



<br>





      service_worker_registration_id, kEntryPrefix,



<span class="line"><!---->      service_worker_registration_id, kEntryPrefix,<!----></span>



<br>





      base::BindOnce(&ContentIndexDatabase::DidGetDescriptions,



<span class="line"><!---->      base::BindOnce(&amp;ContentIndexDatabase::DidGetDescriptions,<!----></span>



<br>





                     weak_ptr_factory_core_.GetWeakPtr(),



<span class="line"><!---->                     weak_ptr_factory_core_.GetWeakPtr(),<!----></span>



<br>





                     service_worker_registration_id, std::move(callback)));



<span class="line"><!---->                     service_worker_registration_id, std::move(callback)));<!----></span>



<br>





"""



<span class="line"><!---->"""<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





But as you can see, it only take the id of service worker. This is an untrust arguments as it is from render process. From a compromised renderer process, the attacker can easy guest the |service_worker_registration_id|(as it starts from 0) and enum it from 0 to 1000 etc... So I think we should check the origin as well.



<span class="line"><!---->But as you can see, it only take the id of service worker. This is an untrust arguments as it is from render process. From a compromised renderer process, the attacker can easy guest the |service_worker_registration_id|(as it starts from 0) and enum it from 0 to 1000 etc... So I think we should check the origin as well.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This will lead to the attacker can get the information about content index descriptions from all origins which users accessed before.



<span class="line"><!---->This will lead to the attacker can get the information about content index descriptions from all origins which users accessed before.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





On the other hand, another interface |Delete| seems like has the same problems.



<span class="line"><!---->On the other hand, another interface |Delete| seems like has the same problems.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





how to reproduce:



<span class="line"><!---->how to reproduce:<!----></span>



<br>





$python ./copy_mojo_js_bindings.py /path/to/chrome/.../out/Debug/gen



<span class="line"><!---->$python ./copy_mojo_js_bindings.py /path/to/chrome/.../out/Debug/gen<!----></span>



<br>





$out/Debug/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS  '



<span class="line"><!---->$out/Debug/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS  '<!----></span>





http://localhost:8000/victim.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000/victim.html"><!---->http://localhost:8000/victim.html<!----></a>





'



<span class="line"><!---->'<!----></span>



<br>





$out/Debug/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS  '



<span class="line"><!---->$out/Debug/chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS  '<!----></span>





http://localhost:8001/attacker.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8001/attacker.html"><!---->http://localhost:8001/attacker.html<!----></a>





'



<span class="line"><!---->'<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





port 8000/victim.html is used for add a description for content index.



<span class="line"><!---->port 8000/victim.html is used for add a description for content index.<!----></span>



<br>





port 8001/attacker.html is used for stole the other origin content index description.



<span class="line"><!---->port 8001/attacker.html is used for stole the other origin content index description.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

I'm running into issues with getting this to repro. Here are the steps I took to try to repro this:



<span class="line"><!---->I'm running into issues with getting this to repro. Here are the steps I took to try to repro this:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





0. Build chrome in outdir ~/chromium/src/out_linux/Release



<span class="line"><!---->0. Build chrome in outdir ~/chromium/src/out_linux/Release<!----></span>



<br>





1. Extract PoC.zip and cd into the directory.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Extract PoC.zip and cd into the directory.<!----></span>



<br>





2. Run `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py ~/chromium/src/out_linux/Release/gen/`



<span class="line"><!---->2. Run `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py ~/chromium/src/out_linux/Release/gen/`<!----></span>



<br>





3. In a first terminal, run `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8000`.



<span class="line"><!---->3. In a first terminal, run `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8000`.<!----></span>



<br>





4. In a second terminal, run `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8001`.



<span class="line"><!---->4. In a second terminal, run `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8001`.<!----></span>



<br>





5. In a third terminal, run `mkdir /tmp/crbug1244568`, then cd into ~/chromium/src/ and run `./out_linux/Release/chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/crbug1244568 --enable-blink-features=MojoJS "



<span class="line"><!---->5. In a third terminal, run `mkdir /tmp/crbug1244568`, then cd into ~/chromium/src/ and run `./out_linux/Release/chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/crbug1244568 --enable-blink-features=MojoJS "<!----></span>





http://localhost:8000/victim.html"`



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000/victim.html&quot;`"><!---->http://localhost:8000/victim.html"`<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





This loads the URL in a tab but the renderer immediately gets killed with RESULT_CODE_KILLED_BAD_MESSAGE which seems like it's running afoul of Mojo message validation.  Reloading the page seems to work.



<span class="line"><!---->This loads the URL in a tab but the renderer immediately gets killed with RESULT_CODE_KILLED_BAD_MESSAGE which seems like it's running afoul of Mojo message validation.  Reloading the page seems to work.<!----></span>



<br>

It doesn't make this seem infeasible in practice, I just found it curious enough to warrant further investigation :-)

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
